    Dash (-) = No data reported.
    NA = Not available.
    W   = Withheld to avoid disclosure of individual company data.



   Notes:  Values through 1980 reflect the month of reporting; values since then
reflect the month of acquisition, which can be the month of loading, the month
of landing, or sometime between those events.  Prices for crude oil can be
determined at a time other than the acquisition date.  See the Explanatory Notes
section for additional detail.
  Notes:  Values for the current 2 months are preliminary. Values shown for
previous months are revised. Data are final upon publication in the  Petroleum
Marketing Annual.
  1 Includes sales through retail outlets as well as all direct sales to end
users that were not made through company-operated retail outlets, e.g., sales to
agricultural customers, commercial sales, and industrial sales.
  Sources:  Energy Information Administration Forms EIA-782A, "Refiners'/Gas
Plant Operators' Monthly Petroleum Product Sales Report," and EIA-782B,
"Resellers'/Retailers' Monthly Petroleum Product Sales Report."
